ReFrame logs

1. ReFrame scheduler script

#!/bin/bash
#SBATCH --job-name="rfm_RegressionTest_26677fa6"
#SBATCH --ntasks=128
#SBATCH --ntasks-per-node=128
#SBATCH --cpus-per-task=1
#SBATCH --output=rfm_job.out
#SBATCH --error=rfm_job.err
#SBATCH --exclusive
#SBATCH --partition=public
#SBATCH --threads-per-core=1
#SBATCH --time=0-00:30:0
source /etc/profile.d/modules.sh
export PATH=/opt/apptainer/v1.3.5/apptainer/bin/:$PATH
mpiexec -n 128 -bind-to core apptainer exec -B"/data/cemosis/github-actions-runner/actions-runner-1/_work/bench.ktirio.fr/bench.ktirio.fr/build/reframe/stage/gaya/public/default/RegressionTest_26677fa6:/rfm_workdir" --home /data/cemosis/benchmark --bind /data/cemosis/benchmark/input_data:/input_data --env OMP_NUM_THREADS=1 --sharens --bind /opt/:/opt/ /data/cemosis/github-actions-runner/actions-runner-1/_work/bench.ktirio.fr/bench.ktirio.fr/kub.sif feelpp_kub_cem --config-files /input_data/kub/idealHeaters.cfg --cem.simulator.lod0.modelisation.maxfloors=10 --cem.simulator.sun.filename=/input_data/kub/simulators/Sun.fmu --cem.gis.metadata.filename=/input_data/kub/Paris/vegetation/2km/gis.json --cem.mesh.lod0.filename=/input_data/kub/Paris/vegetation/2km//mesh_0_Lod0.msh --cem.weather.filename=/input_data/kub/Paris/weather.csv --cem.scenarios.filename=/input_data/kub/scenarios_local/scenarios.json --cem.instance.time.start=0 --cem.instance.time.stop=86400 --cem.instance.time.step=3600 --cem.instance.postprocess.export.visualization.enabled=true --cem.instance.postprocess.export.report.enabled=true --cem.instance.postprocess.export.outputs.csv.enabled=false --cem.instance.postprocess.export.outputs.enabled=true --cem.instance.solar_shading.enabled=true --cem.instance.idealflows.enabled=true --cem.database.directory /data/cemosis/benchmark/kub/26677fa6/Paris_Berlin --directory /data/cemosis/benchmark/kub/26677fa6/Paris_Berlin
